\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Set the end-\/of-\/file reached callback. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\subsection{Detailed Description}
Placing and receiving calls. 

The \doxyref{Linphone\+Call}{p.}{group__call__control_gac0a4861d7c4702c64f7106f2b893c69e} object represents an incoming or outgoing call managed by the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a}. Outgoing calls can be created using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+invite()}{p.}{group__call__control_gaaea662739cc3825eaa80d8ac264a883c} or \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+invite\+\_\+address()}{p.}{group__call__control_gaac6720bef666db932ae77e07c2201b4c}, while incoming calls are notified to the application through the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table\+::call\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed}{p.}{struct__LinphoneCoreVTable_a771c633cfce7bae2cc0160fbd377bf28} callback.

See the basic call \doxyref{tutorial}{p.}{group__basic__call__tutorials}.

\subsubsection{Linphone\+Call\+Cbs}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \+\_\+\+Linphone\+Call\+Cbs \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Cbs}}



That class holds all the callbacks which are called by Linphone\+Call objects. 

Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+factory\+\_\+create\+\_\+call\+\_\+cbs()}{p.}{group__initializing_gab6e69c9eae9550424929a48bb8570015} to create an instance. Then, call the callback setters on the events you need to monitor and pass the object to a Linphone\+Call instance through \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+add\+\_\+callbacks()}{p.}{group__call__misc_gaeffe3718b5b59d9614fc2ff26ae35273}. \mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga541b93049ea73c5b548350fecb28a7fe}}

Linphone\+Privacy\+Id&rfc3325 The presence of this privacy type in a Privacy header field indicates that the user would like the Network Asserted Identity to be kept private with respect to S\+IP entities outside the Trust Domain with which the user authenticated. \index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept}}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept an incoming call. 

Basically the application is notified of incoming calls within the call\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} structure, where it will receive a Linphone\+Call\+Incoming event with the associated Linphone\+Call object. The application can later accept the call using this method. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga447f3caa41ebdf6a9cef01c599d623b0}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept an early media session for an incoming call. 

This is identical as calling \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_gae7252bc7a303a5155f276ca4ca4b8a57} with N\+U\+LL parameters. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_gae7252bc7a303a5155f276ca4ca4b8a57} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gae7252bc7a303a5155f276ca4ca4b8a57}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



When receiving an incoming, accept to start a media session as early-\/media. 

This means the call is not accepted but audio \& video streams can be established if the remote party supports early media. However, unlike after call acceptance, mic and camera input are not sent during early-\/media, though received audio \& video are played normally. The call can then later be fully accepted using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga560e5223603ddd425a06e945e177dbdb} or \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga0a39c513c2e89cdddd034195342befbd}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & The call parameters to use (can be N\+U\+LL) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gac1b2a3f049a2351195d54035db63c789}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept call modifications initiated by other end. 

This call may be performed in response to a \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state notification. When such notification arrives, the application can decide to call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga3de5b75cc14f8f4f768cfbdcca2a3342} so that it can have the time to prompt the user. \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+remote\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga65b4ca2f01d684019f6ae5621eb430f6} can be used to get information about the call parameters requested by the other party, such as whether a video stream is requested.

When the user accepts or refuse the change, \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gac1b2a3f049a2351195d54035db63c789} can be done to answer to the other party. If params is N\+U\+LL, then the same call parameters established before the update request will continue to be used (no change). If params is not N\+U\+LL, then the update will be accepted according to the parameters passed. Typical example is when a user accepts to start video, then params should indicate that video stream should be used (see \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga195ed008fbb19ded55070bb149e72ec5}). 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & A Linphone\+Call\+Params object describing the call parameters to accept \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise (actually when this function call is performed outside ot \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga0a39c513c2e89cdddd034195342befbd}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+with\+\_\+params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept an incoming call, with parameters. 

Basically the application is notified of incoming calls within the call\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} structure, where it will receive a Linphone\+Call\+Incoming event with the associated Linphone\+Call object. The application can later accept the call using this method. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & The specific parameters for this call, for example whether video is accepted or not. Use N\+U\+LL to use default parameters \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+cancel\+\_\+dtmfs()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+cancel\+\_\+dtmfs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Stop current D\+T\+MF sequence sending. 

Please note that some D\+T\+MF could be already sent, depending on when this function call is delayed from \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+send\+\_\+dtmfs}{p.}{group__call__control_ga581ba26014845861b8b4c91dc4643d25}. This function will be automatically called if call state change to anything but Linphone\+Call\+Streams\+Running.

\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga3de5b75cc14f8f4f768cfbdcca2a3342}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



When receiving a \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state notification, prevent Linphone\+Core from performing an automatic answer. 

When receiving a \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state notification (ie an incoming re\+I\+N\+V\+I\+TE), the default behaviour of Linphone\+Core is defined by the \char`\"{}defer\+\_\+update\+\_\+default\char`\"{} option of the \char`\"{}sip\char`\"{} section of the config. If this option is 0 (the default) then the Linphone\+Core automatically answers the re\+I\+N\+I\+V\+TE with call parameters unchanged. However when for example when the remote party updated the call to propose a video stream, it can be useful to prompt the user before answering. This can be achieved by calling \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gad2b1c660f288100da56016e28639a106} during the call state notification, to deactivate the automatic answer that would just confirm the audio but reject the video. Then, when the user responds to dialog prompt, it becomes possible to call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gac1b2a3f049a2351195d54035db63c789} to answer the re\+I\+N\+V\+I\+TE, with eventually video enabled in the Linphone\+Call\+Params argument.

The \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} notification can also arrive when receiving an I\+N\+V\+I\+TE without S\+DP. In such case, an unchanged offer is made in the 200\+Ok, and when the A\+CK containing the S\+DP answer is received, \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} is triggered to notify the application of possible changes in the media session. However in such case defering the update has no meaning since we just generating an offer.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 if the \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga3de5b75cc14f8f4f768cfbdcca2a3342} was done outside a valid \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} notification 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gaeb063497e0a73274d16f9fe63cb40baa}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const char$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the Z\+R\+TP authentication token to verify. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

Returns whether Z\+R\+TP authentication token is verified. 

If not, it must be verified by users as described in Z\+R\+TP procedure. Once done, the application must inform of the results with \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+set\+\_\+authentication\+\_\+token\+\_\+verified()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga3ce1e87718e88df21bca4a19b6e80967}.

{\em call} & the Linphone\+Call \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+UE if authentication token is verifed, false otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Call}$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+replaced\+\_\+call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the call object this call is replacing, if any. 

Call replacement can occur during call transfers. By default, the core automatically terminates the replaced call and accept the new one. This function allows the application to know whether a new incoming call is a one that replaces another one. \mbox{\label{group__call__control_gaed6336c031d02f6b4ca5cf3373367214}}

\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{cp,  }\item[{bool\+\_\+t}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Indicate low bandwith mode. 

Configuring a call to low bandwidth mode will result in the core to activate several settings for the call in order to ensure that bitrate usage is lowered to the minimum possible. Typically, ptime (packetization time) will be increased, audio codec\textquotesingle{}s output bitrate will be targetted to 20kbit/s provided that it is achievable by the codec selected after S\+DP handshake. Video is automatically disabled. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em cp} & Linphone\+Call\+Params object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em enabled} & A boolean value telling whether to activate the low bandwidth mode or not. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga195ed008fbb19ded55070bb149e72ec5}}

\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+local\+\_\+conference\+\_\+mode@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+local\+\_\+conference\+\_\+mode}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+local\+\_\+conference\+\_\+mode@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+local\+\_\+conference\+\_\+mode}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+local\+\_\+conference\+\_\+mode()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool\+\_\+t linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+local\+\_\+conference\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{cp }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Tell whether the call is part of the locally managed conference. 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
If a conference server is used to manage conferences, that function does not return T\+R\+UE even if the conference is running.~\newline
 If you want to test whether the conference is running, you should test whether \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+conference()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga12ce79dfd0095fb41915f273e8b39e03} return a non-\/null pointer. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em cp} & Linphone\+Call\+Params object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A boolean value telling whether the call is part of the locally managed conference. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Get the session name of the media session (ie in S\+DP). 

Subject from the S\+IP message can be retrieved using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+get\+\_\+custom\+\_\+header()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga35ff99ed72925d1160706adf8ce89325} and is different.

\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gac3f7643e84b1afcfdcdcb6a19d821409}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth\+\_\+enabled@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth\+\_\+enabled}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth\+\_\+enabled@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth\+\_\+enabled}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth\+\_\+enabled()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool\+\_\+t linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth\+\_\+enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{cp }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Tell whether the call has been configured in low bandwidth mode or not. 

This mode can be automatically discovered thanks to a stun server when activate\+\_\+edge\+\_\+workarounds=1 in section [net] of configuration file. An application that would have reliable way to know network capacity may not use activate\+\_\+edge\+\_\+workarounds=1 but instead manually configure low bandwidth mode with \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+low\+\_\+bandwidth()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga7f442dd06cba9bb1065ee759e204b206}. When enabled, this param may transform a call request with video in audio only mode. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em cp} & Linphone\+Call\+Params object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A boolean value telling whether the low bandwidth mode has been configured/detected. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Refine bandwidth settings for this call by setting a bandwidth limit for audio streams. 

As a consequence, codecs whose bitrates are not compatible with this limit won\textquotesingle{}t be used.

\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+set\+\_\+record\+\_\+file@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+set\+\_\+record\+\_\+file}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+set\+\_\+record\+\_\+file@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+set\+\_\+record\+\_\+file}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+set\+\_\+record\+\_\+file()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+set\+\_\+record\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{cp,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{path }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable recording of the call. 

This function must be used before the call parameters are assigned to the call. The call recording can be started and paused after the call is established with \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+start\+\_\+recording()}{p.}{group__call__misc_gaa92c7b4c3443ff4ae29f7b57f57cfd35} and linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+pause\+\_\+recording(). 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em cp} & Linphone\+Call\+Params object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em path} & A string containing the path and filename of the file where audio/video streams are to be written. The filename must have either .mkv or .wav extention. The video stream will be written only if a M\+KV file is given. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gabc82ea0fde212db0ca3db1936cbeab37}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{refer\+\_\+to }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs a simple call transfer to the specified destination. 

The remote endpoint is expected to issue a new call to the specified destination. The current call remains active and thus can be later paused or terminated. It is possible to follow the progress of the transfer provided that transferee sends notification about it. In this case, the transfer\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} is invoked to notify of the state of the new call at the other party. The notified states are \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Init}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaae99727dfb0a8e30ef04ff96ce3bf7e36} , \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Progress}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa4f6c8b38f68a9bdfdd6d59cc904f924c}, \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Ringing}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa229cfe72a8dfee15bdae9f2125b43c67} and \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Connected}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa1a32cc3919ca3658eed7deebadbe13b9}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call to be transfered \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em refer\+\_\+to} & The destination the call is to be refered to \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga80ce41f9e1bb41ac20930cbb64f875f8}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{dest }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Transfers a call to destination of another running call. 

This is used for \char`\"{}attended transfer\char`\"{} scenarios. The transfered call is supposed to be in paused state, so that it is able to accept the transfer immediately. The destination call is a call previously established to introduce the transfered person. This method will send a transfer request to the transfered person. The phone of the transfered is then expected to automatically call to the destination of the transfer. The receiver of the transfer will then automatically close the call with us (the \textquotesingle{}dest\textquotesingle{} call). It is possible to follow the progress of the transfer provided that transferee sends notification about it. In this case, the transfer\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} is invoked to notify of the state of the new call at the other party. The notified states are \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Init}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaae99727dfb0a8e30ef04ff96ce3bf7e36} , \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Progress}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa4f6c8b38f68a9bdfdd6d59cc904f924c}, \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Ringing}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa229cfe72a8dfee15bdae9f2125b43c67} and \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Connected}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa1a32cc3919ca3658eed7deebadbe13b9}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A running call you want to transfer \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dest} & A running call whose remote person will receive the transfer \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gaf01d64f1d6d38d91658e0d00050fe6bd}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+unref@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+unref}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+unref@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+unref}!Call control@{Call control}}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gafc43150942cd163d5ec46828a17df237}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Updates a running call according to supplied call parameters or parameters changed in the Linphone\+Core. 

In this version this is limited to the following use cases\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item setting up/down the video stream according to the video parameter of the Linphone\+Call\+Params (see \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga195ed008fbb19ded55070bb149e72ec5} ).
\item changing the size of the transmitted video after calling \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+preferred\+\_\+video\+\_\+size()}{p.}{group__media__parameters_ga7b7dd1b5e086b268dbd05f393f9402af} In case no changes are requested through the Linphone\+Call\+Params argument, then this argument can be omitted and set to N\+U\+LL. W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG\+: Updating a call in the Linphone\+Call\+Paused state will still result in a paused call even if the media directions set in the params are sendrecv. To resume a paused call, you need to call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+resume()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga29f896fa60c1055590d7329fa74963d0}.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A Linphone\+Call object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & The new call parameters to use (may be N\+U\+LL) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga8a263459d37ab14422ac2080279a0435}}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+video()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{float}]{zoom\+\_\+factor,  }\item[{float $\ast$}]{cx,  }\item[{float $\ast$}]{cy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Perform a zoom of the video displayed during a call. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em call} & the call. \\
\hline
{\em zoom\+\_\+factor} & a floating point number describing the zoom factor. A value 1.\+0 corresponds to no zoom applied. \\
\hline
{\em cx} & a floating point number pointing the horizontal center of the zoom to be applied. This value should be between 0.\+0 and 1.\+0. \\
\hline
{\em cy} & a floating point number pointing the vertical center of the zoom to be applied. This value should be between 0.\+0 and 1.\+0.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
cx and cy are updated in return in case their coordinates were too excentrated for the requested zoom factor. The zoom ensures that all the screen is fullfilled with the video. \mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga9f40474789a57f1a10f167647b1531a6}}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept an incoming call. 

Basically the application is notified of incoming calls within the call\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} structure, where it will receive a Linphone\+Call\+Incoming event with the associated Linphone\+Call object. The application can later accept the call using this method. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The Linphone\+Call object representing the call to be answered \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga560e5223603ddd425a06e945e177dbdb} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga880a2b5dd66710fe1f8a3e2dcf793f63}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept call modifications initiated by other end. 

This call may be performed in response to a \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state notification. When such notification arrives, the application can decide to call linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update\+\_\+call() so that it can have the time to prompt the user. \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+get\+\_\+remote\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga65b4ca2f01d684019f6ae5621eb430f6} can be used to get information about the call parameters requested by the other party, such as whether a video stream is requested.

When the user accepts or refuse the change, \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga880a2b5dd66710fe1f8a3e2dcf793f63} can be done to answer to the other party. If params is N\+U\+LL, then the same call parameters established before the update request will continue to be used (no change). If params is not N\+U\+LL, then the update will be accepted according to the parameters passed. Typical example is when a user accepts to start video, then params should indicate that video stream should be used (see \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga195ed008fbb19ded55070bb149e72ec5}). 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call for which to accept an update \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & A Linphone\+Call\+Params object describing the call parameters to accept \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise (actually when this function call is performed outside ot \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gac1b2a3f049a2351195d54035db63c789} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga8972d13671b880d3b4de047da5e64ac4}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accept an incoming call, with parameters. 

Basically the application is notified of incoming calls within the call\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} structure, where it will receive a Linphone\+Call\+Incoming event with the associated Linphone\+Call object. The application can later accept the call using this method. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The Linphone\+Call object representing the call to be answered \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & The specific parameters for this call, for example whether video is accepted or not. Use N\+U\+LL to use default parameters \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



When receiving an incoming, accept to start a media session as early-\/media. 

This means the call is not accepted but audio \& video streams can be established if the remote party supports early media. However, unlike after call acceptance, mic and camera input are not sent during early-\/media, though received audio \& video are played normally. The call can then later be fully accepted using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call()}{p.}{group__call__control_gaebf3fdd612ce71b3a317a0213245acfb} or \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga8972d13671b880d3b4de047da5e64ac4}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call to accept \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & The call parameters to use (can be N\+U\+LL) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+accept\+\_\+early\+\_\+media\+\_\+with\+\_\+params()}{p.}{group__call__control_gae7252bc7a303a5155f276ca4ca4b8a57} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+decline\+\_\+call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Reason}}]{reason }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\label{group__call__control_gad2b1c660f288100da56016e28639a106}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



When receiving a \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state notification, prevent Linphone\+Core from performing an automatic answer. 

When receiving a \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} state notification (ie an incoming re\+I\+N\+V\+I\+TE), the default behaviour of Linphone\+Core is defined by the \char`\"{}defer\+\_\+update\+\_\+default\char`\"{} option of the \char`\"{}sip\char`\"{} section of the config. If this option is 0 (the default) then the Linphone\+Core automatically answers the re\+I\+N\+I\+V\+TE with call parameters unchanged. However when for example when the remote party updated the call to propose a video stream, it can be useful to prompt the user before answering. This can be achieved by calling \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gad2b1c660f288100da56016e28639a106} during the call state notification, to deactivate the automatic answer that would just confirm the audio but reject the video. Then, when the user responds to dialog prompt, it becomes possible to call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+accept\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga880a2b5dd66710fe1f8a3e2dcf793f63} to answer the re\+I\+N\+V\+I\+TE, with eventually video enabled in the Linphone\+Call\+Params argument.

The \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} notification can also arrive when receiving an I\+N\+V\+I\+TE without S\+DP. In such case, an unchanged offer is made in the 200\+Ok, and when the A\+CK containing the S\+DP answer is received, \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} is triggered to notify the application of possible changes in the media session. However in such case defering the update has no meaning since we just generating an offer.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call for which to defer the update \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 if the \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+defer\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gad2b1c660f288100da56016e28639a106} was done outside a valid \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Updated\+By\+Remote}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaad51ee049c7dee729776ef5bc76ddb2c2} notification
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+defer\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga3de5b75cc14f8f4f768cfbdcca2a3342} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga392ce3ed50a75e50fa9efac73fcae890}}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+calls()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const bctbx\+\_\+list\+\_\+t$\ast$ linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+get\+\_\+calls (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current list of calls. 

Note that this list is read-\/only and might be changed by the core after a function call to \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+iterate()}{p.}{group__initializing_ga7bdac8ac386483fc4e0876e4c5d13755}. Similarly the Linphone\+Call objects inside it might be destroyed without prior notice. To hold references to Linphone\+Call object into your program, you must use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+ref()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga6d0a37f1d1fb23eed31491cfe546cd01}.

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & The Linphone\+Core object \\

Indicates whether the local participant is part of a conference. 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
That function automatically fails in the case of conferences using a conferencet server (focus). If you use such a conference, you should use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+conference\+\_\+remove\+\_\+participant()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga17c115720548a536d73dd584f5dc97bc} instead. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+pause\+\_\+call()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+pause\+\_\+call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Pauses the call. 

If a music file has been setup using \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+play\+\_\+file()}{p.}{group__media__parameters_ga14a0bf3c9d8ad451574c41ae71eb03cc}, this file will be played to the remote user. The only way to resume a paused call is to call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+resume\+\_\+call()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga4748ae709cad319911494c957cc7e2b8}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call to pause \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+from\+\_\+conference@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+from\+\_\+conference}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+from\+\_\+conference@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+from\+\_\+conference}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+from\+\_\+conference()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+remove\+\_\+from\+\_\+conference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Remove a call from the conference. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lc} & the linphone core \\
\hline
{\em call} & a call that has been previously merged into the conference.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
After removing the remote participant belonging to the supplied call, the call becomes a normal call in paused state. If one single remote participant is left alone together with the local user in the conference after the removal, then the conference is automatically transformed into a simple call in Streams\+Running state. The conference\textquotesingle{}s resources are then automatically destroyed.

In other words, unless \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+leave\+\_\+conference()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga2922c6f870b37e480fd1d3b07138eec9} is explicitly called, the last remote participant of a conference is automatically put in a simple call in running state.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+sound\+\_\+resources\+\_\+locked()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool\+\_\+t linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+sound\+\_\+resources\+\_\+locked (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Check if a call will need the sound resources in near future (typically an outgoing call that is awaiting response). 

In liblinphone, it is not possible to have two independant calls using sound device or camera at the same time. In order to prevent this situation, an application can use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+sound\+\_\+resources\+\_\+locked()}{p.}{group__call__control_gaddcb4be3bee7cc9e89330541a176b106} to know whether it is possible at a given time to start a new outgoing call. When the function returns T\+R\+UE, an application should not allow the user to start an outgoing call. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A boolean value telling whether a call will need the sound resources in near future 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Terminate the running conference. 

If it is a local conference, all calls inside it will become back separate calls and will be put in \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Paused}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa59c57a8b9a7a0086a79c85028bb4cefc} state. \index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{refer\+\_\+to }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs a simple call transfer to the specified destination. 

The remote endpoint is expected to issue a new call to the specified destination. The current call remains active and thus can be later paused or terminated. It is possible to follow the progress of the transfer provided that transferee sends notification about it. In this case, the transfer\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} is invoked to notify of the state of the new call at the other party. The notified states are \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Init}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaae99727dfb0a8e30ef04ff96ce3bf7e36} , \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Progress}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa4f6c8b38f68a9bdfdd6d59cc904f924c}, \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Ringing}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa229cfe72a8dfee15bdae9f2125b43c67} and \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Connected}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa1a32cc3919ca3658eed7deebadbe13b9}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call to be transfered \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em refer\+\_\+to} & The destination the call is to be refered to \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer()}{p.}{group__call__control_gabc82ea0fde212db0ca3db1936cbeab37} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga6d75f4e938b36260e906f93b7885cfab}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call\+\_\+to\+\_\+another@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call\+\_\+to\+\_\+another}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call\+\_\+to\+\_\+another@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call\+\_\+to\+\_\+another}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call\+\_\+to\+\_\+another()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+call\+\_\+to\+\_\+another (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{dest }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Transfers a call to destination of another running call. 

This is used for \char`\"{}attended transfer\char`\"{} scenarios. The transfered call is supposed to be in paused state, so that it is able to accept the transfer immediately. The destination call is a call previously established to introduce the transfered person. This method will send a transfer request to the transfered person. The phone of the transfered is then expected to automatically call to the destination of the transfer. The receiver of the transfer will then automatically close the call with us (the \textquotesingle{}dest\textquotesingle{} call). It is possible to follow the progress of the transfer provided that transferee sends notification about it. In this case, the transfer\+\_\+state\+\_\+changed callback of the \doxyref{Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table}{p.}{group__initializing_ga1ca71386f318e4044967ddf32ac7aacb} is invoked to notify of the state of the new call at the other party. The notified states are \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Init}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaae99727dfb0a8e30ef04ff96ce3bf7e36} , \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Progress}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa4f6c8b38f68a9bdfdd6d59cc904f924c}, \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Outgoing\+Ringing}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa229cfe72a8dfee15bdae9f2125b43c67} and \doxyref{Linphone\+Call\+Connected}{p.}{group__call__control_ggafc310fd9ba742f7730c632fd72b875eaa1a32cc3919ca3658eed7deebadbe13b9}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & A running call you want to transfer \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dest} & A running call whose remote person will receive the transfer \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+transfer\+\_\+to\+\_\+another()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga80ce41f9e1bb41ac20930cbb64f875f8} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
\mbox{\label{group__call__control_ga5e9fc2d960c07f5ad37efd299a90a474}} 
\index{Call control@{Call control}!linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+update\+\_\+call@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+update\+\_\+call}}
\index{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+update\+\_\+call@{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+update\+\_\+call}!Call control@{Call control}}
\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+update\+\_\+call()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily L\+I\+N\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED \textbf{ Linphone\+Status} linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+update\+\_\+call (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Core} $\ast$}]{lc,  }\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Call} $\ast$}]{call,  }\item[{const \textbf{ Linphone\+Call\+Params} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Updates a running call according to supplied call parameters or parameters changed in the Linphone\+Core. 

In this version this is limited to the following use cases\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item setting up/down the video stream according to the video parameter of the Linphone\+Call\+Params (see \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+params\+\_\+enable\+\_\+video()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga195ed008fbb19ded55070bb149e72ec5} ).
\item changing the size of the transmitted video after calling \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+preferred\+\_\+video\+\_\+size()}{p.}{group__media__parameters_ga7b7dd1b5e086b268dbd05f393f9402af} In case no changes are requested through the Linphone\+Call\+Params argument, then this argument can be omitted and set to N\+U\+LL. W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG\+: Updating a call in the Linphone\+Call\+Paused state will still result in a paused call even if the media directions set in the params are sendrecv. To resume a paused call, you need to call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+resume\+\_\+call()}{p.}{group__call__control_ga4748ae709cad319911494c957cc7e2b8}.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em lc} & Linphone\+Core object \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em call} & The call to be updated \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em params} & The new call parameters to use (may be N\+U\+LL) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if successful, -\/1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item[\textbf{ Deprecated}]Use \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+call\+\_\+update()}{p.}{group__call__control_gafc43150942cd163d5ec46828a17df237} instead \end{DoxyRefDesc}
